NOTE: Spawns of cars are randomised thus same inputs will have different outputs. In this version there are no user input as
this version was used to develope the intersections.
with the same inputs. Also the final grid at the end of the simulatiom will be taken as the output. The output is the 
terminal representation of the simulation, with each second of the simulation bieng displayed over multiple grids.
The 0's represnet empty roads and 1's represent the cars moving right to left and -1 represents cars going left to right. n/a represents the fact that the users did not need to input
those values. A video for the first test case has also been attached.
